<h2 class="h">disturbed</h2> <span class="z">&nbsp;</span> <a id="bbffdd94f53e4ada99d357acd7f69be7"></a><a href="entry://#4339be03a04a4d779dfc0237ea7139bb" class="to-top"><span class="pos">adjective</span></a> </div> <span class="pos-g"><span class="pos">adjective</span></span> <div class="pron-gs ei-g"> <span class="pron-g" geo="br"><span class="prefix">BrE</span> <span class="phon"><span class="bre">BrE</span><span class="separator">/</span><span class="wrap">/</span>dɪ<span class="ptl">ˈstɜːbd</span><span class="wrap">/</span><span class="separator">/</span></span> <a class="sound audio_play_button pron-uk icon-audio" otitle=" pronunciation English" href="sound://media/english/uk_pron/d/dis/distu/disturbed__gb_1.mp3" type="sound"> &nbsp; </a></span> <span href="/topic/unhappiness/disturbed" otitle="Topic Unhappiness"><span class="xr-g"><span class="xh">Unhappiness</span></span></a></span></span> <div class="clear"> &nbsp; </div> <br> </div> </div> <span class="sn-gs"><li class="sn-g"><a href="entry://#4339be03a04a4d779dfc0237ea7139bb" class="sen"></a><span class="num">1</span><span class="def">mentally ill, especially because of very unhappy or shocking experiences</span><span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"> <span class="x">a special school for emotionally disturbed children</span></span><span class="x-g"> <span class="rx-g"><span class="x">His behaviour is deeply disturbed.</span></span></span></span><span class="collapse" otitle="Synonyms"><span class="unbox"> <span class="heading" onclick="if(this.parentNode.className=='unbox'){this.parentNode.className='unbox is-active';}else if(this.parentNode.className=='unbox is-active'){this.parentNode.className='unbox';}">Synonyms</span><span class="body"><span class="h1">mentally ill</span><span class="inline"><span class="li">insane</span> <span class="li">neurotic</span> <span class="li">psychotic</span> <span class="li">disturbed</span> <span class="li">unstable</span></span><span class="p">These words all describe somebody who is suffering from a mental illness.</span><span class="deflist"><span class="li"><span class="eb">mentally ill</span> suffering from an illness of the mind, especially in a way that affects the way you think and behave</span><span class="li"><span class="eb">insane</span> [not usually before noun] (<span class="ei">rather formal</span>) suffering from a serious mental illness and unable to live in normal society:<span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"><span class="rx-g"><span class="x">The question is, was the man insane when he committed the crime?</span></span></span></span> <span class="un">In informal English <span class="eb">insane</span> can describe somebody who is not suffering from a mental illness, but whose mind does not work normally, especially because they are under pressure. This meaning is used especially in the phrases <span class="ei">go insane</span> and <span class="ei">drive somebody insane</span>.</span></span><span class="li"><span class="eb">neurotic</span> (<span class="ei">medical</span>) suffering from or connected with neurosis <span class="gl"><span class="wrap">(</span><span class="prefix">=</span> a mental illness in which a person suffers strong feelings of fear and worry<span class="wrap">)</span></span> :<span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"><span class="x">the treatment of anxiety in neurotic patients</span></span></span> <span class="un">In informal English <span class="eb">neurotic</span> is also used to describe somebody who is not suffering from a mental illness, but is not behaving in a calm way because they are worried about something:<span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"><span class="rx-g"><span class="x">She became neurotic about keeping the house clean.</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="li"><span class="eb">psychotic</span> (<span class="ei">medical</span>) suffering from or connected with psychosis <span class="gl"><span class="wrap">(</span><span class="prefix">=</span> a serious mental illness in which thought and emotions lose connection with external reality<span class="wrap">)</span></span>. <span class="un">In informal English <span class="eb">psychotic</span> is sometimes used to describe anyone suffering from a mental illness, but in correct medical usage it only describes people who have difficulty relating to external reality. It contrasts with <span class="eb">neurotic</span>, which describes people who are less seriously mentally ill and are still able to distinguish what is real from what is not.</span></span><span class="li"><span class="eb">disturbed</span> mentally ill, especially because of very unhappy or shocking experiences:<span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"><span class="rx-g"><span class="x">He works with emotionally disturbed children.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="li"><span class="eb">unstable</span> having emotions and behaviour that are likely to change suddenly and unexpectedly</span></span><span class="h3">Patterns</span><span class="bullet"><span class="li"> neurotic/​psychotic/​disturbed/​unstable <span class="eb">behaviour</span></span><span class="li"> neurotic/​psychotic <span class="eb">illnesses/​disorders/​symptoms/​patients</span></span><span class="li"> <span class="eb">seriously</span> mentally ill/​neurotic/​psychotic/​disturbed</span><span class="li"> <span class="eb">emotionally/​mentally</span> disturbed/​unstable</span></span></span></span></span></li><li class="sn-g"><a href="entry://#4339be03a04a4d779dfc0237ea7139bb" class="sen"></a><span class="num">2</span><span class="def">unhappy and full of bad or shocking experiences</span><span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"> <span class="rx-g"><span class="x">The killer had a disturbed family background.</span></span></span></span></li><li class="sn-g"><a href="entry://#4339be03a04a4d779dfc0237ea7139bb" class="sen"></a><span class="num">3</span><span class="def">very anxious and unhappy about something</span><span class="x-gs"><span class="x-g"> <span class="rx-g"><span class="x">I was deeply disturbed and depressed by the news.</span></span></span></span> </li> <span class="xr-gs"><span class="prefix">compare</span> <a class="Ref" href="entry://undisturbed" otitle="undisturbed definition"><span class="xr-g"><span class="xh">undisturbed</span></span></a></span></span> <span class="res-g"><span class="collapse" otitle="Extra examples"><span class="unbox"><span class="heading" are severely disturbed.</span></span><span class="x-g"> <span class="x">emotionally disturbed children</span></span><span class="x-g"> <span class="x">Some of the people on the ward are very
